3) next.config.mjs  (security headers incl. CSP)

/** @type {import('next').NextConfig} */
const nextConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  async headers() {
    const csp = [
      "default-src 'self'",
      "base-uri 'self'",
      "object-src 'none'",
      "frame-ancestors 'self'",
      "img-src 'self' data: blob:",
      "style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://fonts.googleapis.com",
      "font-src 'self' https://fonts.gstatic.com",
      "script-src 'self' https://js.stripe.com",
      "connect-src 'self' https://api.stripe.com",
      "frame-src 'self' https://js.stripe.com",
      "form-action 'self' https://checkout.stripe.com",
      "upgrade-insecure-requests"
    ].join("; ");
    const security = [
      ["Content-Security-Policy", csp],
      ["Referrer-Policy", "no-referrer"],
      ["X-Content-Type-Options", "nosniff"],
      ["X-Frame-Options", "SAMEORIGIN"],
      ["Permissions-Policy", "camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=()"]
    ].map(([key, value]) =&gt; ({ key, value }));

    return [
      { source: "/(.*)", headers: security }
    ];
  }
};
export default nextConfig;

&gt; Later, remove 'unsafe-inline' after you move any inline styles to CSS files.

4) middleware.js  (simple IP rate-limit)

const WINDOW_MS = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 min
const LIMIT = 300;                // 300 req / window / IP
const buckets = new Map();

export function middleware(req) {
  const url = new URL(req.url);
  // lighter limits for sensitive routes
  const isTight = ["/api/client-log", "/api/checkout"].some(p =&gt; url.pathname.startsWith(p));
  const limit = isTight ? 60 : LIMIT;

  const ip = req.headers.get("x-forwarded-for")?.split(",")[0]?.trim() || "127.0.0.1";
  const now = Date.now();
  const key = `${ip}:${isTight ? "tight" : "gen"}`;
  const b = buckets.get(key) || { reset: now + WINDOW_MS, count: 0 };
  if (now &gt; b.reset) { b.count = 0; b.reset = now + WINDOW_MS; }
  b.count++;
  buckets.set(key, b);

  if (b.count &gt; limit) {
    return new Response("Too many requests. Try later.", {
      status: 429,
      headers: { "Retry-After": "900" }
    });
  }
  return;
}

export const config = {
  matcher: [
    "/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)"
  ]
};

5) pages/api/checkout.js

import Stripe from "stripe";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== "POST") return res.status(405).end("Method Not Allowed");
  try {
    const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);
    const { priceId } = req.body;
    if (!priceId) return res.status(400).json({ error: "Missing priceId" });

    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({
      mode: "payment",
      line_items: [{ price: priceId, quantity: 1 }],
      success_url: `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL}/?success=1`,
      cancel_url: `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL}/?canceled=1`
    });
    res.status(200).json({ url: session.url });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("checkout error:", e);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Unable to create session" });
  }
}

6) pages/api/webhook.js  (raw body + signature verify)

import Stripe from "stripe";

export const config = {
  api: { bodyParser: false } // keep raw body for signature verification
};

function buffer(req) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) =&gt; {
    const chunks = [];
    req.on("data", (c) =&gt; chunks.push(c));
    req.on("end", () =&gt; resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));
    req.on("error", reject);
  });
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== "POST") return res.status(405).end("Method Not Allowed");
  const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);

  const buf = await buffer(req);
  const sig = req.headers["stripe-signature"];
  try {
    const event = stripe.webhooks.constructEvent(
      buf,
      sig,
      process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET
    );

    if (event.type === "checkout.session.completed") {
      const session = event.data.object;
      console.log(" Checkout completed:", session.id, session.amount_total);
      // TODO: grant LMS access, email, etc.
    }
    if (event.type === "payment_intent.succeeded") {
      const pi = event.data.object;
      console.log(" PaymentIntent succeeded:", pi.id, pi.amount);
    }

    res.json({ received: true });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error("Webhook verify error:", err.message);
    res.status(400).send(`Webhook Error: ${err.message}`);
  }
}

7) pages/api/client-log.js  (front-end error sink)

import UAParser from "ua-parser-js";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== "POST") return res.status(405).end("Method Not Allowed");
  try {
    const { level = "error", message = "", stack = "", url = "" } = req.body || {};
    const ua = new UAParser(req.headers["user-agent"]).getResult();
    const id = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
    console.log(` ClientLog#${id} [${level}] ${String(message).slice(0, 2000)}\nURL=${url}\nUA=${ua.browser.name} ${ua.browser.version} on ${ua.os.name}\nSTACK=${String(stack).slice(0, 2000)}`);
    res.json({ ok: true, id });
  } catch {
    res.status(200).json({ ok: true });
  }
}

9) pages/index.js  (demo + client bug catcher)

import { useState } from "react";

export default function Home() {
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);

  const pay = async (priceId) =&gt; {
    try {
      setBusy(true);
      const r = await fetch("/api/checkout", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {"Content-Type":"application/json"},
        body: JSON.stringify({ priceId })
      });
      const { url } = await r.json();
      window.location = url;
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      alert("Could not start checkout.");
    } finally {
      setBusy(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    &lt;main style={{fontFamily:"Inter, system-ui", maxWidth:900, margin:"40px auto", padding:"0 16px"}}&gt;
      &lt;h1&gt;Elevate for Humanity&lt;/h1&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;Secure Stripe Checkout + hardened Next.js starter.&lt;/p&gt;

      &lt;h3&gt;Enroll &amp; Pay&lt;/h3&gt;
      &lt;button disabled={busy} onClick={()=&gt;pay(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DSP || process.env.DSP_PRICE_ID)}&gt;Pay DSP  $4,325&lt;/button&gt; &amp;nbsp;
      &lt;button disabled={busy} onClick={()=&gt;pay(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CPR || process.env.CPR_PRICE_ID)}&gt;Pay CPR  $125&lt;/button&gt;

      &lt;hr style={{margin:"24px 0"}}/&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;&lt;a href="/catalog-and-policies"&gt;Catalog &amp; Policies&lt;/a&gt;  &lt;a href="/api/healthz" target="_blank"&gt;Health&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

      {/* Client-side error reporter */}
      &lt;script dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{__html: `
        (function(){
          function send(level,msg,stack){
            try{fetch('/api/client-log',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify({level:level,message:msg,stack:stack,url:location.href})});}catch(e){}
          }
          window.addEventListener('error',function(e){send('error',e.message||(e.error&amp;&amp;e.error.message)||'Unhandled error', (e.error&amp;&amp;e.error.stack)||'');});
          window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection',function(e){var r=e.reason||{};send('error', r.message||r.toString()||'Unhandled rejection', r.stack||'');});
        })();
      `}}/&gt;
    &lt;/main&gt;
  );
}

  const Box = ({children}) =&gt; &lt;div style={{background:"#fff",border:"1px solid #ece7ff",borderRadius:12,padding:16,boxShadow:"0 6px 18px rgba(25,7,79,.06)"}}&gt;{children}&lt;/div&gt;;

          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Delivery&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Hybrid (online LMS + live labs)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Total Cost&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;b&gt;$4,325&lt;/b&gt;  Tuition $3,500 + Fees/Supplies $825&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Credential&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;DSP Certificate (provider-issued)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Admissions&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;18+; HS Diploma/GED; government ID; background check (healthcare)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Outcomes&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Person-centered supports; documentation; safety; ethics; communication; med assist (per scope)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Pathways&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;DSP, Home Health Aide, Residential Support Staff&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
        &lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
      &lt;/Box&gt;&lt;br/&gt;

      &lt;Box&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;CPR &amp; Emergency Response&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;table&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Length&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;16 hours (2 sessions)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Delivery&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;In-person with live instructor&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Total Cost&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;b&gt;$125&lt;/b&gt; (includes supplies and manikin use)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Credential&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;AHA CPR Card&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Admissions&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;16+; government-issued ID&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Outcomes&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;BLS skills; AED; choking rescue; basic first aid&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Pathways&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Healthcare support; childcare; public safety&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
        &lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
      &lt;/Box&gt;&lt;br/&gt;

      &lt;Box&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Business Startup &amp; Marketing&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;table&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Length&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;60 hours (68 weeks)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Delivery&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Hybrid (workshops + LMS)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Total Cost&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;b&gt;$1,200&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Credential&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Certiport Entrepreneurship &amp; Small Business (ESB)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Admissions&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;16+; basic computer literacy&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Outcomes&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Registration; budgeting/funding; digital marketing; sales funnels&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Pathways&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Entrepreneur; marketing assistant; freelancer&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
        &lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
      &lt;/Box&gt;

      &lt;p style={{background:"#fff8e6",border:"1px solid #f4d27d",padding:12,borderRadius:10,marginTop:10}}&gt;
        Printable copy: &lt;a href="/static/Elevate_Student_Handbook_and_Catalog.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"&gt;Download Student Handbook &amp; Catalog (PDF)&lt;/a&gt;
      &lt;/p&gt;

      &lt;H2&gt;Student Handbook &amp; Policies&lt;/H2&gt;
      &lt;Box&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Admissions&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;ul&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;18+; High School Diploma or GED (program-specific)&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;Valid government-issued ID&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;Background check &amp; drug screen for healthcare/public safety programs&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;Orientation completion prior to start&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;/ul&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Attendance&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;Minimum &lt;b&gt;85%&lt;/b&gt; of scheduled hours required to earn credentials. Tardiness (&amp;gt;15 minutes) may be recorded as absent. Make-ups within 14 days where available.&lt;/p&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Academic Progress / Completion&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;Minimum &lt;b&gt;70%&lt;/b&gt; on knowledge assessments and successful demonstration of all required skills. Some credentials require a third-party exam.&lt;/p&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Refund &amp; Withdrawal Policy&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;ul&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;100%&lt;/b&gt; refund if withdrawal occurs before the first day of class.&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;50%&lt;/b&gt; refund if within the first instructional week.&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;&lt;b&gt;No refunds&lt;/b&gt; after the first week. (CPR: 100% refund with 24-hour notice; else non-refundable.)&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;/ul&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Grievance / Complaint Process&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;ol&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;Submit a written complaint to your Instructor.&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;If unresolved, escalate to the Program Director at &lt;a href="mailto:info@elevateforhumanity.org"&gt;info@elevateforhumanity.org&lt;/a&gt;. Acknowledgment within 10 business days; resolution target within 30 business days.&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;If still unresolved, you may appeal to Indiana DWD/DOE per state guidance.&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;/ol&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;ADA / Section 504 Accommodations&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;Reasonable accommodations are available. Submit requests in writing before the start date or when a need arises.&lt;/p&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Non-Discrimination / EO&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;We do not discriminate on the basis of race, color, national origin, sex, age, disability, religion, or status. &lt;b&gt;Auxiliary aids and services are available upon request for individuals with disabilities.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
        &lt;h3&gt;Code of Conduct&lt;/h3&gt;
        &lt;ul&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;Professional behavior, safety compliance, and respectful communication&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;No harassment, violence, or substance use on premises&lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;li&gt;Academic integrity; proper use of LMS resources and equipment&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;/ul&gt;
      &lt;/Box&gt;

      &lt;H2&gt;Compliance &amp; Consumer Info&lt;/H2&gt;
      &lt;Box&gt;
        &lt;table&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Completion Rate&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Collecting &amp; validating current cohort data (available upon request).&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Job Placement Rate&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Collecting &amp; validating current cohort data (available upon request).&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Funding Options&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;WIOA, WRG, JRI, employer sponsorships, scholarships (where available).&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Delivery&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Hybrid or in-person with live instruction; LMS login provided.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
          &lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Equal Opportunity Statement&lt;/th&gt;&lt;td&gt;Elevate for Humanity is an equal opportunity training provider. Auxiliary aids and services are available upon request for individuals with disabilities.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;
        &lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;
      &lt;/Box&gt;

      &lt;h2 style={{color:"#6b46c1", marginTop:24}}&gt;Contact&lt;/h2&gt;
      &lt;Box&gt;
        &lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Email:&lt;/b&gt; &lt;a href="mailto:info@elevateforhumanity.org"&gt;info@elevateforhumanity.org&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;
           &lt;b&gt;Phone:&lt;/b&gt; &lt;a href="tel:+13173143757"&gt;(317) 314-3757&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;
           &lt;b&gt;Address:&lt;/b&gt; Indianapolis, IN
        &lt;/p&gt;
      &lt;/Box&gt;
    &lt;/main&gt;
  );
}


---

How to use on Replit (quick)

1. Create a Node.js (Next.js) repl, add the files above.


2. Set Secrets (.env.local values) in Replit.


3. Install &amp; run: npm i then npm run dev (or npm run start after npm run build).


4. In Stripe  Developers  Webhooks  Add endpoint:
https://&lt;your-replit-domain&gt;/api/webhook
Select events: checkout.session.completed, payment_intent.succeeded.


5. Test an Enroll &amp; Pay button (DSP/CPR). Real payments require Live Mode and sk_live/pk_live.




---

If youd rather stick with plain Express instead of Next.js, say the word and Ill give you the strict-CSP Express version (no inline scripts/styles) to drop into your current Replit.

aria-disabled="true" role="textbox">Awesome  heres a Next.js + Stripe hardened starter you can drop into Replit.
It includes: secure headers, rate-limiting, Stripe Checkout, verified webhooks (raw body), input hardening, a client-side error logger, /healthz, and a sample Catalog &amp; Policies page.


---

 File tree (copy exactly)

.
 .env.local              # put your secrets here (Replit: Secrets)
 next.config.mjs         # security headers (CSP, etc.)
 middleware.js           # lightweight IP rate limit
 pages
   index.js             # demo homepage with 2 Enroll &amp; Pay buttons
   catalog-and-policies.js
   api
      checkout.js       # creates Stripe Checkout Session
      webhook.js        # Stripe webhook (raw body + signature verify)
      client-log.js     # receives client error logs
      healthz.js        # uptime probe
 package.json

  },

3) next.config.mjs  (security headers incl. CSP)

/** @type {import('next').NextConfig} */
const nextConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  async headers() {
    const csp = [
      "default-src 'self'",
      "base-uri 'self'",
      "object-src 'none'",
      "frame-ancestors 'self'",
      "img-src 'self' data: blob:",
      "style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://fonts.googleapis.com",
      "font-src 'self' https://fonts.gstatic.com",
      "script-src 'self' https://js.stripe.com",
      "connect-src 'self' https://api.stripe.com",
      "frame-src 'self' https://js.stripe.com",
      "form-action 'self' https://checkout.stripe.com",
      "upgrade-insecure-requests"
    ].join("; ");
    const security = [
      ["Content-Security-Policy", csp],
      ["Referrer-Policy", "no-referrer"],
      ["X-Content-Type-Options", "nosniff"],
      ["X-Frame-Options", "SAMEORIGIN"],
      ["Permissions-Policy", "camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=()"]
    ].map(([key, value]) =&gt; ({ key, value }));

    return [
      { source: "/(.*)", headers: security }
    ];
  }
};
export default nextConfig;

&gt; Later, remove 'unsafe-inline' after you move any inline styles to CSS files.




---

4) middleware.js  (simple IP rate-limit)

const WINDOW_MS = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 min
const LIMIT = 300;                // 300 req / window / IP
const buckets = new Map();

export function middleware(req) {
  const url = new URL(req.url);
  // lighter limits for sensitive routes
  const isTight = ["/api/client-log", "/api/checkout"].some(p =&gt; url.pathname.startsWith(p));
  const limit = isTight ? 60 : LIMIT;

  const ip = req.headers.get("x-forwarded-for")?.split(",")[0]?.trim() || "127.0.0.1";
  const now = Date.now();
  const key = `${ip}:${isTight ? "tight" : "gen"}`;
  const b = buckets.get(key) || { reset: now + WINDOW_MS, count: 0 };
  if (now &gt; b.reset) { b.count = 0; b.reset = now + WINDOW_MS; }
  b.count++;
  buckets.set(key, b);

  if (b.count &gt; limit) {
    return new Response("Too many requests. Try later.", {
      status: 429,
      headers: { "Retry-After": "900" }
    });
  }
  return;
}

export const config = {
  matcher: [
    "/((?!_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)"
  ]
};


---

5) pages/api/checkout.js

import Stripe from "stripe";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== "POST") return res.status(405).end("Method Not Allowed");
  try {
    const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);
    const { priceId } = req.body;
    if (!priceId) return res.status(400).json({ error: "Missing priceId" });

    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({
      mode: "payment",
      line_items: [{ price: priceId, quantity: 1 }],
      success_url: `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL}/?success=1`,
      cancel_url: `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL}/?canceled=1`
    });
    res.status(200).json({ url: session.url });
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("checkout error:", e);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Unable to create session" });
  }
}


---

6) pages/api/webhook.js  (raw body + signature verify)

import Stripe from "stripe";

export const config = {
  api: { bodyParser: false } // keep raw body for signature verification
};

function buffer(req) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) =&gt; {
    const chunks = [];
    req.on("data", (c) =&gt; chunks.push(c));
    req.on("end", () =&gt; resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));
    req.on("error", reject);
  });
}

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== "POST") return res.status(405).end("Method Not Allowed");
  const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);

  const buf = await buffer(req);
  const sig = req.headers["stripe-signature"];
  try {
    const event = stripe.webhooks.constructEvent(
      buf,
      sig,
      process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET
    );

    if (event.type === "checkout.session.completed") {
      const session = event.data.object;
      console.log(" Checkout completed:", session.id, session.amount_total);
      // TODO: grant LMS access, email, etc.
    }
    if (event.type === "payment_intent.succeeded") {
      const pi = event.data.object;
      console.log(" PaymentIntent succeeded:", pi.id, pi.amount);
    }

    res.json({ received: true });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error("Webhook verify error:", err.message);
    res.status(400).send(`Webhook Error: ${err.message}`);
  }
}


---

7) pages/api/client-log.js  (front-end error sink)

import UAParser from "ua-parser-js";

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method !== "POST") return res.status(405).end("Method Not Allowed");
  try {
    const { level = "error", message = "", stack = "", url = "" } = req.body || {};
    const ua = new UAParser(req.headers["user-agent"]).getResult();
    const id = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
    console.log(` ClientLog#${id} [${level}] ${String(message).slice(0, 2000)}\nURL=${url}\nUA=${ua.browser.name} ${ua.browser.version} on ${ua.os.name}\nSTACK=${String(stack).slice(0, 2000)}`);
    res.json({ ok: true, id });
  } catch {
    res.status(200).json({ ok: true });
  }
}

export default function handler(req, res) {

9) pages/index.js  (demo + client bug catcher)

import { useState } from "react";

export default function Home() {
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false);

  const pay = async (priceId) =&gt; {
    try {
      setBusy(true);
      const r = await fetch("/api/checkout", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {"Content-Type":"application/json"},
        body: JSON.stringify({ priceId })
      });
      const { url } = await r.json();
      window.location = url;
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
      alert("Could not start checkout.");
    } finally {
      setBusy(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    &lt;main style={{fontFamily:"Inter, system-ui", maxWidth:900, margin:"40px auto", padding:"0 16px"}}&gt;
      &lt;h1&gt;Elevate for Humanity&lt;/h1&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;Secure Stripe Checkout + hardened Next.js starter.&lt;/p&gt;

      &lt;h3&gt;Enroll &amp; Pay&lt;/h3&gt;
      &lt;button disabled={busy} onClick={()=&gt;pay(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DSP || process.env.DSP_PRICE_ID)}&gt;Pay DSP  $4,325&lt;/button&gt; &amp;nbsp;
      &lt;button disabled={busy} onClick={()=&gt;pay(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_CPR || process.env.CPR_PRICE_ID)}&gt;Pay CPR  $125&lt;/button&gt;

      &lt;hr style={{margin:"24px 0"}}/&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;&lt;a href="/catalog-and-policies"&gt;Catalog &amp; Policies&lt;/a&gt;  &lt;a href="/api/healthz" target="_blank"&gt;Health&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

      {/* Client-side error reporter */}
      &lt;script dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{__html: `
        (function(){
          function send(level,msg,stack){
            try{fetch('/api/client-log',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify({level:level,message:msg,stack:stack,url:location.href})});}catch(e){}
          }
          window.addEventListener('error',function(e){send('error',e.message||(e.error&amp;&amp;e.error.message)||'Unhandled error', (e.error&amp;&amp;e.error.stack)||'');});
          window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection',function(e){var r=e.reason||{};send('error', r.message||r.toString()||'Unhandled rejection', r.stack||'');});
        })();
      `}}/&gt;
    &lt;/main&gt;
  );
}

---

How to use on Replit (quick)

1. Create a Node.js (Next.js) repl, add the files above.


2. Set Secrets (.env.local values) in Replit.


3. Install &amp; run: npm i then npm run dev (or npm run start after npm run build).


4. In Stripe  Developers  Webhooks  Add endpoint:
https://&lt;your-replit-domain&gt;/api/webhook
Select events: checkout.session.completed, payment_intent.succeeded.


5. Test an Enroll &amp; Pay button (DSP/CPR). Real payments require Live Mode and sk_live/pk_live.




---

If youd rather stick with plain Express instead of Next.js, say the word and Ill give you the strict-CSP Express version (no inline scripts/styles) to drop into your current Replit.
